<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пообещать.html>пообеща́вший</a> (3152)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пообещать.html>пообеща́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poobeščávšij</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пообещать.html>пообеща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poobeščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***поп.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>поп</a> (4274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">попъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">popŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παπάς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">papás</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, variant of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πάππας</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">páppas</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">daddy, papa</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">попа́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">popád-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попадать.html>попада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hit (a target)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:попадать.html>попада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>цель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>popadátʹ</b> v celʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to miss (one's aim)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get (to), to come (upon), to fall (into), to find oneself (in), to hit (upon)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попадать.html>попада́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popadátʹ</b> komú-libo v rúki</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to fall into somebody's hands</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попадать.html>попада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:домой.html>домо́й</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popadátʹ</b> domój</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to get home</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попадать.html>попада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плена.html>плен</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popadátʹ</b> v plen</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to be taken prisoner</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попадать.html>попада́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">popadátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попадаться.html>попада́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popadátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасться.html>попа́сться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get caught</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come across, to chance (up)on, to meet</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попадать.html>попада́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">popadátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попадать.html>попада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hit (a target)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>цель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>popástʹ</b> v celʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to miss (one's aim)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>popálo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">anyhow, at random, haphazard, any which way (<i>idiomatic</i>)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to get (to), to come (upon), to fall (into), to find oneself (in), to hit (upon)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popástʹ</b> komú-libo v rúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into somebody's hands</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:домой.html>домо́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popástʹ</b> domój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get home</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плена.html>плен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>popástʹ</b> v plen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be taken prisoner</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">popástʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасться.html>попа́сться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">popástʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попадаться.html>попада́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get caught</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come across, to chance (up)on, to meet</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">popástʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>па́сть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 7b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:попадаться.html>попада́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-попас-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***поперек.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поперек.html>поперек</a> (4228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*перёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*perjók</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crosswise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Underlying root found in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">перекъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perekŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">width, crossbeam</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> as well as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">пе́рек</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjérjek</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">пере́ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peréka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">contradiction</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">прѣкꙑ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prěky</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">пря́ко</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prjáko</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straight, across</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">при̏јек</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">steep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">при̏јекӣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straight, nearest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">при̏јеко</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">through</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">prek</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">adverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">preko</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">prèk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">preposition</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">příka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">steepness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">příč</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">width</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">priek</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">resistance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">w poprzek</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across, crosswise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or obsolete <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">przeko</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">prěki</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">pŕeki</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***попереть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:попереть.html>попере́ть</a> (13361)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переть.html>пере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попереть.html>попере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poperétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to push forward, to barge <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">through</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:попереть.html>попере́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозь.html>сквозь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толпа.html>толпу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poperétʹ</b> skvozʹ tolpú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to barge through the crowd</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:против.html>про́тив</a> () <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попереть.html>попрёшь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prótiv () ne poprjóšʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you have to face (); there's nothing you can do (with)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour out, to flow out, to erupt, to gush out, to burst forth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лава.html>ла́ва</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:попереть.html>попёрла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вершина.html>верши́ны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вулкан.html>вулка́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">láva <b>popjórla</b> iz veršíny vulkána</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:лава.html>lava</a> erupted [burst forth] from the top of the volcano</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злоба.html>зло́ба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:попереть.html>попёрла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zlóba tak i <b>popjórla</b> iz nevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he burst with fury</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удача.html>уда́ча</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:попереть.html>попёрла</a></b> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">udáča <b>popjórla</b> komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">someone has a windfall; someone has a big/lucky break</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">luck <b>gushed out</b> for someone</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to push/thrust/chuck/turn/drive out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to haul</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***поперечный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поперечный.html>попере́чный</a> (10969)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">поперёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poperjók</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">across</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поперечный.html>попере́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poperéčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cross-
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поперечный.html>попере́чное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сечение.html>сече́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poperéčnoje</b> sečénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cross-section</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>transverse, crosswise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречный.html>встре́чный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поперечный.html>попере́чный</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">káždyj vstréčnyj i <b>poperéčnyj</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">any Tom, Dick or Harry, anyone</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">anyone oncoming or crosswise</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>lateral</li></ol>
